\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
detail namespace with internal helper functions 

This namespace collects functions that should not be exposed, implementations of some \doxylink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json} methods, and meta-\/programming helpers.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}\index{detail@{detail}!value\_t@{value\_t}}
\index{value\_t@{value\_t}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{value\_t}{value\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632} 
enum class \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{detail::\+value\+\_\+t}} :\+ std::\+uint8\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



the JSON type enumeration 

This enumeration collects the different JSON types. It is internally used to distinguish the stored values, and the functions basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+null(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+object(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+array(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+string(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+boolean(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+number() (with basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+number\+\_\+integer(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+number\+\_\+unsigned(), and basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+number\+\_\+float()), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+discarded(), basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+primitive(), and basic\+\_\+json::\+is\+\_\+structured() rely on it.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
There are three enumeration entries (number\+\_\+integer, number\+\_\+unsigned, and number\+\_\+float), because the library distinguishes these three types for numbers:\+ basic\+\_\+json::\+number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t is used for unsigned integers, basic\+\_\+json::\+number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t is used for signed integers, and basic\+\_\+json::\+number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t is used for floating-\/point numbers or to approximate integers which do not fit in the limits of their respective type.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see basic\+\_\+json::\+basic\+\_\+json(const value\+\_\+t value\+\_\+type) -- create \doxylink{json_8hpp_a1d1d2369d6b815e0f2e1f281efe0039d}{a} JSON \doxylink{namespacedetail_a6334559c220a676ac4b953ea342f85ce}{value} with the default \doxylink{namespacedetail_a6334559c220a676ac4b953ea342f85ce}{value} \doxylink{_durango_2_iggy_2gdraw_2gdraw__d3d1x__shared_8inl_ad3b279bec4f11ba3839421e2018d1f63}{for} \doxylink{json_8hpp_a1d1d2369d6b815e0f2e1f281efe0039d}{a} given type
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

String\+Type detail::\+escape (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String\+Type}]{s}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



string escaping as described in RFC 6901 (Sect. 4) 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em s} & string to escape \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
escaped string
\end{DoxyReturn}
Note the order of escaping "{}\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}"{} to "{}\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}0"{} and "{}/\+"{} to "{}\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}1"{} is important.

std::\+size\+\_\+t detail::\+hash (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_common_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} Basic\+Json\+Type \&}]{j}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



hash a JSON value 

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} hash function tries to rely on std::\+hash where possible. Furthermore, the type of the JSON value is taken into account to have different hash values for null, 0, 0U, and false, etc.

\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_aac7ca91589afb0bad68baec5949daaa2}\index{detail@{detail}!operator$<$@{operator$<$}}
\index{operator$<$@{operator$<$}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator$<$()}{operator<()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacedetail_aac7ca91589afb0bad68baec5949daaa2} 
bool detail::\+operator$<$ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_common_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{value\+\_\+t}}}]{lhs}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_common_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{value\+\_\+t}}}]{rhs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



comparison operator for JSON types 

Returns an ordering that is similar to Python:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item order:\+ null \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} boolean \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} number \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} object \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} array \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} string \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} binary
\item furthermore, each type is not smaller than itself
\item discarded values are not comparable
\item binary is represented as a b"{}"{} string in python and directly comparable to a string; however, making a binary array directly comparable with a string would be surprising behavior in a JSON file.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{replace\_substring()}{replace\_substring()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacedetail_a6fd295e53b1dd4f46e235e6afee26d5e} 
template$<$typename String\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_durango_2_miles_2include_2mss_8h_afed5b2f9cfdce0d76b8a9e307d336b91}{void}} detail::\+replace\+\_\+substring (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String\+Type \&}]{s}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_common_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} String\+Type \&}]{f}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_common_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} String\+Type \&}]{t}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



replace all occurrences of a substring by another string 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in,out}}  & {\em s} & the string to manipulate; changed so that all occurrences of {\itshape f} are replaced with {\itshape t} \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em f} & the substring to replace with {\itshape t} \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em t} & the string to replace {\itshape f} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} search string {\itshape f} must not be empty. {\bfseries{This precondition is enforced with an assertion.}}
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a3f0588f1a546b169113e6e1e293168f4}\index{detail@{detail}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacedetail_a3f0588f1a546b169113e6e1e293168f4} 
template$<$typename Float\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{json_8hpp_a5f2aaec3b681d0a72f7d6e90b70cdcd1}{JSON\+\_\+\+HEDLEY\+\_\+\+RETURNS\+\_\+\+NON\+\_\+\+NULL}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} detail::\+to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{first}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_common_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{last}{, }\item[{Float\+Type}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



generates a decimal representation of the floating-\/point number value in \+[first, last). 

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} format of the resulting decimal representation is similar to printf\textquotesingle{}s g format. Returns an iterator pointing past-\/the-\/end of the decimal representation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} input number must be finite, i.\+e. NaN\textquotesingle{}s and Inf\textquotesingle{}s are not supported. 

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} buffer must be large enough. 

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} result is NOT null-\/terminated. 
\end{DoxyNote}
